# Kolektibilitas Piutang

Kolektibilitas piutang menggambarkan efektivitas Perseroan dalam menagih pembayaran dari pelanggan atau mitra usaha. Untuk menjaga kelancaran arus kas, Perseroan terus berupaya menc Gatkan kolektibilitas secara konsisten setiap tahuna. Rincian piutang untuk 2 tahun terakhir diuraikan sebagai berikut.

The debt-to-equity ratio was recorded at 0.82 times in 2024, a decrease from 0.91 times in 2023. The debt-to-assets ratio also declined, from 0.48 times in 2023 to 0.45 times in 2024. Meanwhile, the debt-to-sales ratio increased to 0.27 times in 2024, compared to 0.17 times in the previous year.

# Receivables Collectibility

The collectibility of receivables describes the effectiveness of the Company in collecting payments from customers or business partners. To maintain a smooth cash flow, the Company continues to strive to increase collectibility consistently every year. The details of receivables for the last 2 years are described as follows.

# Kebijakan Manajemen atas Struktur Modal

Perseroan menerapkan kebikan pengelolaan struktur modal yang seimbang antara utang dan ekuitas untuk mendukung keberlanjutan bisnis jangka panjang dan meminimalkan risiko keuang. Manajemen rutin memantau rasio keuang, yaitu rasio utang terhadap ekuitas, serta mempertimbangkan kondisi ekonomi, risiko bisnis, dan peluang investasi dalam menentukan kebikan terkait modal, dividen, ata pembiayaan. Kebikan ini dirancang untuk menjaga fleksilitas keuang, mendukung pengembangan usaha, dan memberikan nilai tambah bagi Pemegang Saham{serta pemangku kepada mengenungan secara berkelanjutan.

# Management Policy on Capital Structure

The Company implements a balanced capital structure management policy between debt and equity to support long-term business sustainability and minimize financial risks. Management routinely monitors the financial ratio, which is the ratio of debt to equity, as well as considering economic conditions, business risks, and investment opportunities in determining policies related to capital, dividends, or financing. This policy is designed to maintain financial flexibility, support business development, and provide added value for Shareholders and stakeholders on a sustainable basis.

# PROSPEK USAHA

BUSINESS PROSPECT

Prospek sektor informasi dan komunikasi Indonesia di 2025 didorong oleh inovasi tekologi speerti 5G, Al, dan IoT yang mencatingkatan efisiensi layanan digital. Selain itu, pendanaan yang mencatingkat pada sektor tekologi dan informasi, terutama pada startup tekologi, seda dukungan kebujakan pemerintah, speerti Proyek Strategis Nasional (PSN), mempercepat perkembangan sektor ini. Peningkatan jumlah pengguna internet juga membruka peluangistar bagi ekonomi digital. Dengan prospek tersebut, Direksi yakin Perseroan dapat memanfaatkan peluang yang ada untuk mencapai pertumbuhan yang lebih optimal.

The prospects of Indonesia's information and communication sector in 2025 are driven by technological innovations such as 5G, AI, and IoT that increase the efficiency of digital services. In addition, increased funding in the technology and information sector, especially in technology startups, as well as government policy support, such as the National Strategic Project (PSN), accelerates the development of this sector. The increase in the number of internet users also opens up great opportunities for the digital economy. With this prospect, the Board of Directors believes that the Company can take advantage of the existing opportunities to achieve more optimal growth.

# KEBIJAKAN DAN PEMBAGIAN DIVIDEN

POLICY AND DIVIDEND DISTRIBUTION

# Kebijakan Dividen

Perseroan seksutif, perakutuk dan pembagian dividien dalam Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham (RUPS) dengan mempertimbangkan kebujakan internal, peraturan yang berlaku, Anggaran Dasar, dan usulan Pemegang Saham. Proses pembagian dividien ini menjadi tanggung jawab Direksi, yang memastikan pelaksanaannya sesuai dengan kepada jangka panjang Perseroan dan kesehatan keuangan.

# Pembagian Dividen

Merujuk pada keputusan RUPS Tahunan yang diselenggakaran pada 5 Juni 2024, Pemegang Saham menyetujui pembagian dividun tunai sebesar Rp2,46 miliar. Pembagian dividen tersebut telah dilakukan oleh Direksi sesuai dengan prosedur dan kebikan yang berlaku.

# Dividend Policy

The Company distributes dividends in the General Meeting of Shareholders (GMS) by considering internal policies, applicable regulations, Articles of Association, and Shareholders' proposals. The process of distributing dividends is the responsibility of the Board of Directors, which ensures that its implementation is in accordance with the Company's long-term interests and financial health.

# Dividend Distribution

Referring to the decision of the Annual General Meeting of Shareholders held on June 5, 2024, Shareholders agreed to distribute cash dividends of Rp2,46 billion. The dividend distribution has been carried out by the Board of Directors in accordance with the applicable procedures and policies.

# PERUBAHAN KEBIJAKAN AKUNTANSI

ACCOUNTING POLICY CHANGES

Dewan Standar Akuntansi Keuangan Ikatan Akuntan Indonesia (DSAK-IAI) telah menerbitkan amendem dan interpretasi yang berlaku efektif mulai 1 Januari 2024 sebagai berikut.

- Kerangka Standar Pelaporan Keuangan Indonesia (KSPKI) dan perubahan nomor PSAK dan ISAK dalam Standar Akuntansi Keuangan Indonesia (sebelumnya Standar Akuntansi Keuangan), berlaku efektif tanggal 1 Januari 2024. KSPKI mengatur pilar SAK yang berlaku di Indonesia, kriteria, dan perdindahan antar pilar SAK, sedangkan perubahan nomenklatur mengatur ketentuan penomoran PSAK dan ISAK yang mencaku pada IFRS Accounting Standards;  
- Amendemen PSAK 201 "Penyajian Laporan Keuangan tersebut Klasifikasi Liabilitas sebagai Jangka Pendek kepada Jangka Panjang";  
- Amendemen PSAK 116: "Sewa" terkait Liabilititas Sewa pada Transaksi Jual dan Sewa-Balik; dan  
- Amendemen PSAK 207, "Laporan Arus Kas" dan PSAK 107, "Instrumen Keuangan: Pengungkapan" tersebut "Pengaturan Pembiayaan Pemasok."

Penerapan dari amendemen atas standar di atas tidak menimbulkan perubahan substansial atas kebikan akuntansi Perseroan dan tidak memiliki dampak signifikan terhadap Laporan Keuangan pada tahun berjalan atha tahun sebelumnya.

The Financial Accounting Standards Board of the Indonesian Institute of Accountants (DSAK-IAI) has issued amendments and interpretations that will be effective starting January 1, 2024, as follows.

- The Indonesian Financial Reporting Standard Framework (KSPKI) and the changes in the nomenclature of PSAK and ISAK in the Indonesian Financial Accounting Standards (previously known as Financial Accounting Standards) will take effect on January 1, 2024. KSPKI regulates the pillars of SAK applicable in Indonesia, the criteria, and the transition between SAK pillars, while the changes in numbers govern the numbering provisions of PSAK and ISAK that refer to IFRS Accounting Standards;  
- Amendment to PSAK 201 "Presentation of Financial Statements on the Classification of Liabilities as Short Term or Long Term;"  
- Amendment to PSAK 116: "Leases" regarding lease liabilities in sale and leaseback transactions; and  
- Amendments to PSAK 207: "Statements of Cash Flow" and PSAK 107, "Financial Instrument: Disclosure" regarding "Supplier Financing Regulations."

The implementation of the amendment to the above standards does not result in substantial changes to the Company's accounting policies and does not have a significant impact on the financial statements for the current year or the previous year.

# Penetrasi Pasar

The company continues to penetrate the market for the products it currently has, especially for cellular-related products. The company is currently the majority vendor for PT Indosat Tbk (which is also the mobile operator Three after the merger with Hutchinson 3 Indonesia), going forward the company will penetrate the market by trying to become a permanent supplier to other cellular operators such as Telkomsel and XL Axiata. Until now, the Company has been registered as a potential permanent supplier on the Telkomsel Procurement Application system as of September 22, 2022 and has been registered on the Zambia Telecommunications "E-tendering platform" as of September 28, 2022. Until now, the Company has not obtained an agreement or been appointed as permanent supplier by Telkomsel and Zambia Telecomuniation, because the company has not participated in the tender process held by the two.

# Peningkatan Produkt

# Product Improvement

Perseroan Juda berusaha untuk menjadi peningkatan Produk yang telah dimilikinya saat ini, baik secarakasitas, fungsi maupun jangkauan. Hal ini dilakuan antara lain dengan menclngkatkan fungsi dari SIM Card yang tidak希望大家digunakan untuk telepon dan sambungan internet, namun dapat juga digunakan sebagai penyambung komunikasi pada mesin atas peralan atas sebagai tracking device, di industriuperti keuangan dan perbankan (alat pereima pembayaran berbentuk mesin Electronic Data Capture/EDC), manufaktur, dan transportasi/logistik.

The company is also trying to improve the products it currently has, both in terms of capacity, function and range. This is done, among others, by increasing the function of the SIM Card which is not only used for telephone and internet connection, but can also be used as a communication connector on machines or equipment or as a tracking device, in industries such as finance and banking (payment devices in the form of electronic machines). Data Capture/EDC), manufacturing, and transportation/logistics.

# Pengembangan Produk/Jasa Baru

# Development Of New Products/Services

Perseroan akan makalkanan pengembangan Produk bara, terutama pada bisnis IT dan solution, di mana Perseroan secara ini telah mengembangkanproduk/jasa solusi untuk perbankan,produk application/server based yang ditujukan pada perbankan, serta pengembangan solusi bagi untuk Smart Card:seperti penambahan modul analytics, cloud, and mobility.

The company will develop new products, especially in the IT and solution business, where the company is currently developing product/service solutions for banking, Application/server based products aimed at banking, as well as developing new solutions for Smart Cards: such as adding the Analytics module, Cloud and Mobility.

# Diversifikasi Usaha

# Business Diversification

Selain produit Smart Card dan jasa enterprise dan supply chain solution yang telah Perseroan miliki saat, Perseroan berencana untuk menambah kapabilitas Tim IT untuk ke depannya dapat mengembangkanProduk dan jasa yang berhubungan dengan IoT, security solution, serta businessintelligence dan analytics, Seeingga dapat mendiversifikasi Produk dan pelangan di kemudian hari.

In addition to the smart card products and enterprise services and supply chain solutions that the Company currently has, the Company plans to increase the capabilities of the IT team so that in the future they can develop products and services related to the IoT, security solutions, as well as business intelligence and analytics, so that can diversify its products and customers in the future.

# TATA KELOLA  
PERUSAHAAN

GOOD CORPORATE GOVERNANCE

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/a7d6584e-3da5-4f06-974f-1dd224e68ae8/0418143ff2a3a48fafe5f2b37c53e06690c94b68f306830d2c683da797f30372.jpg)

# KOMITMEN GCG

# GCG COMMITMENT

Penerapan tata kelola perusahaan yang baik oleh good corporate governance (GCG) merupakan landasan fundamental bagi Perseroan dalam menjalankan seluruh aktivitas bisnis dengan baik, transparan, dan bertanggung jawab. Dengan mematuhi prinsip-prinsip GCG, Perseroan memastikan operasional usaha senantiasa berada dalam koridor kepadauhan terhadap ketentuan dan peraturan perdang-undangan yang berlaku, serta menghindari potensi risiko yang dapat merugikan perusahaan maupun pemangku kepentingan.

Lebih dari sekadar kepadahan,;penerapan GCG juga berfungsi sebagai instrumen strategis untuk mewujudkan keberlanjutan usaha (sustainability) dalam jangka panjang. Melalui tata kelola yang kuat, Perseroan Berkomitmen untuk menciptakan dan mempertahankan nilai tambah bagi Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya.

# PRINSIP-PRINSIP GCG

# GCG PRINCIPLES

Perseroan mencaku pada prinsip-prinsip GCG yang dikembangkan oleh Komite Nasional Kebijakan Governansi (KNKG) dalam Pedoman Umum Governansi Corporat Indonesia (PUGKI) 2021. Prinsip-prinsip tersebut dijelaskan sebagai berikut.

The implementation of good corporate governance (GCG) is the fundamental foundation for the Company in carrying out all business activities properly, transparently, and responsibly. By complying with the principles of GCG, the Company ensures that business operations are always within the corridor of compliance with applicable provisions and regulations, as well as avoiding potential risks that can harm the company and stakeholders.

More than just compliance, the implementation of GCG also functions as a strategic instrument to realize business sustainability in the long term. Through strong governance, the Company is committed to creating and maintaining added value for Shareholders and other stakeholders.

The Company refers to the principles of GCG developed by the National Governance Policy Committee (KNKG) in the General Guidelines for Indonesian Corporate Governance (PUGKI) 2021. These principles are explained as follows.

# Perilaku Beretika Ethical Behavior

Perseroan senantiasa menginedepankan keujurana, memperlakukan semua pihak dengan hormat (respect), memenuhi komitmen, membrangun serta menjaga nilainilai moral dan kepercayaan secara konsisten. Perseroan juga memerhatikan kepentingan Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya berdasarkan asas kewajaran dan kesetaraan (fairness) dan dikelola secara independen Seeingga masing-masing organ Perseroan tidak saling mendominasi dan tidak dapat diintervensi oleh pihak lainnya.

The Company always prioritizes honesty, treats all parties with respect, fulfills commitments, builds and maintains moral values and beliefs consistently. The Company also pays attention to the interests of Shareholders and other stakeholders based on the principles of fairness and is managed independently so that each organ of the Company does not dominate each other and cannot be intervened by other parties.

# Akuntabilitas Accountability

Perseroan dapat mempertanggungjawabkan kinerjanya secara transparan dan wajar. Untuk itu, Perseroan harus dikelola dengan benar, terukur, dan seksuai dengan kepentingan korporat dengan tetap mempertimbangkan kepentingan Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepentingan. Akuntabilitas merupakan prasyarat yang diperlukan untuk mencapai kinerja yang berkelanjutan.

The Company can account for its performance transparently and fairly. For this reason, the Company must be managed correctly, measurably, and in accordance with corporate interests while considering the interests of Shareholders and stakeholders. Accountability is a necessary prerequisite for achieving sustainable performance.

# Transparansi Transparency

Untuk menjaga obyektivitas dalam menjalankan bisnis, Perseroan menyediakan informasi yang material dan relevan dengan cara yang mudah diakses dan dipahami oleh pemangku kepentingan. Perseroan mengambilinisiatif untuk mengungkapkan tidak dengan masalah yang diisyaratan oleh peraturan perundang-undangan, tetapi juga hal yang penting untuk pengambilan keputusan oleh Pemegang Saham, kreditur, dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya.

To maintain objectivity in conducting business, the Company provides material and relevant information in a way that is easily accessible and understood by stakeholders. The Company takes the initiative to disclose not only issues hinted by laws and regulations, but also matters that are important for decision making by Shareholders, creditors, and other stakeholders

# Keberlanjutan Sustainability

Perseroan mematuhi peraturan perdang-undangan dan Berkomitmen melaksanan tanggung jawab terhadap masyarakat dan lingkungan, agar berkontribusi pada pembangunan berkelanjutan melalui kerja sama dengan semua pemangku kepentingan erkait untuk mencxingkatkan kehidupan yang selaras dengan kepentingan bisnis dan agenda pembangunan berkelanjutan.

The Company complies with laws and regulations and is committed to carrying out its responsibility towards society and the environment, in order to contribute to sustainable development through cooperation with all relevant stakeholders to improve lives in line with business interests and the sustainable development agenda.

# STRUKTUR GCG

# GCG STRUCTURE

Perseroan senantiasa berupaya menerapkan dan mencatingkatkan praktik GCG secara efektif. Upaya ini diwujudkan melalui pembentukan struktur GCG yang mengaku pada Undang-Undang No. 40 Tahun 2007tentang Perseroan Terbatas serta peraturan kerkait lainnya. Struktur ini mencakup Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham (RUPS), Dewan Komisaris, Direksi, Komite Audit, Sekretaris Perusahaan, dan Unit Audit Internal, di mana masingmasing memiliki tugas dan tanggung jawab seksuai ketentuan yang berlaku.

The Company always strives to implement and improve GCG practices effectively. This effort is realized through the formation of the GCG structure which refers to Law No. 40 of 2007 concerning Limited Liability Companies and other related regulations. This structure includes the General Meeting of Shareholders (GMS), Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, Audit Committee, Company Secretary, and Internal Audit Unit, where each has duties and responsibilities according to the applicable provisions.

# PENERAPAN PEDOMAN TATA KELOLA PERUSAHAAN TERBUKA

# IMPLEMENTATION OF PUBLIC COMPANY GOVERNANCE GUIDELINES

Perseroan menerapkan tata kelola berpedoman pada Surat Edaran No. 32/SEOJK.04/2015 yang menjelaskan terkait aspek, prinsip, rekomendasi, dengan uraian sebagai berikut.

The Company implements governance guided by Circular Letter No. 32/SEOJK.04/2015 which explains related aspects, principles, recommendations, with the following description.

<table><tr><td>No.</td><td>Aspek/Prinsip/Rekomendasi

# RAPAT UMUM PEMEGANG SAHAM

# GENERAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS

Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham (RUPS) merupakan kegiatan wajib yang dilaksanakan oleh Perseroan untuk melaporkan telah kinerja selama hari ini dengan Persekitaran. Persekitaran mengelakukan RUPS Tahunan paling lambat 6 bulan setelah berakhirnya tahun buku. Selain itu, Perseroan dapat mengadakan RUPS Luar Biasa secara insidential sesuai kebutuhan dan kepada orang untuk pengambilan keputusan oleh Pemegang Saham, Dewan Komisaris, akan Direksi.

# Pelaksanaan RUPS 2024

Perseroan nutzen RUPS Tahunan dan 1 kali RUPS Luar Biasa pada tanggal 5 Juni 2024, berlokasi di The Belleza Suites Permata Hijau, JI. Soepono No. 34, Permata Hijau, Jakarta Selatan. Uraiantering pelaksanaan RUPS Perseroan di tahun 2024 diungkapkan sebagai berikut.

The General Meeting of Shareholders (RUPS) is a mandatory activity carried out by the Company to report performance results for one period to Shareholders. The Company must hold an Annual General Meeting of Shareholders no later than 6 months after the end of the financial year. In addition, the Company can hold an Extraordinary General Meeting of Shareholders incidentally according to the needs and interests of decision-making by Shareholders, Board of Commissioners, or Board of Directors.

# 2024 GMS Implementation

The Company held the Annual General Meeting of Shareholders and 1 Extraordinary General Meeting of Shareholders on June 5, 2024, located at The Bellezza Suites Permata Hijau JI. Soepeno No. 34, Permata Hijau, South Jakarta. The description related to the implementation of the Company's General Meeting of Shareholders in 2024 is disclosed as follows.

# Agenda RUPS

# RUPS Tahunan

1. Persetujuan Laporan Tahunan dan Laporan Keuangan Tahunan.  
2. Persetujuan penggunaan laba bersih.  
3. Persetujuan atas penetrapan gaji dan/atau honorariumserta tunjangan untuk tahun buku 2024 serta tantiem untuk tahun buku 2023 kepada anggota Direksi dan Dewan Komisaris Perseroan.  
4. Persetujuan penunjukkan akuntan publik dan/atau kantor akuntan publik.

# Agenda RUPS Luar Biasa

1. Perubahan Pasal 17 ayat 5 Anggaran Dasar mengai pengumuman Laporan Keuangan Perseroan.

# Agenda GMS

# Agenda of the Annual GMS

1. Approval of the Annual Report and Annual Financial Statements.  
2. Approval of the allocation of net profit.  
3. Approval of the determination of salaries and/or honoraria as well as allowances for the 2024 financial year and bonuses for the 2023 financial year for members of the Board of Directors and Board of Commissioners of the Company.  
4. Approval of the appointment of a public accountant and/or public accounting firm.

# Agenda of the Extraordinary GMS

1. Amendment to Article 17 paragraph 5 of the Articles of Association regarding the publication of the Company's Financial Statements.

# Keputusan dan Realisasi RUPS Tahunan 5 Juni 2024

Menetapkan gaji dan tunjangan lainnya bagi Dewan Komisaris Perseroan secara keseluruhan untuk tahun buku 2024, dalam jumiah yang sama dengan jumiah gaji dan tunjangan lainnya yang diberikan pada tahun buku 2023, oleh apabila ada kenaikan makai jumiah kenaikannya tidak melebihi 10% dari jumiah gaji dan tunjangan lainnya yang diberikan pada tahun buku 2023, oleh memberikan wewenang kepada Rapat Dewan Komisaris untuk menetapkan alokasinya, dengan memerharitan rekomendasi dari Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi.b. To set the salary and other allowances for the Board of Commissioners of the Company as a whole for the 2024 financial year, in the same amount as the salary and other allowances provided in the 2023 financial year, or, if there is an increase, the increase shall not exceed 10% of the salary and other allowances provided in the 2023 financial year, and to grant authority to the Board of Commissioners' Meeting to determine the allocation, taking into account recommendations from the Nomination and Remuneration Committee.b. # DEWAN KOMISARIS

# BOARD OF COMMISSIONERS

Dewan Komisaris berperan dalam menjalankan fungsi pengawasanuminium memberikan nasihat, saran, dan rekomendasi kepada Direksi terkait pengelolaan dan pengurusan Perseroan secara keseluruhan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Pedoman kerja Dewan Komisaris merujuk pada Anggaran Dasar dan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014tentang Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Emiten atop Perusahaan Publik.

# Criteria [IDX-G.06]

Dewan Komisaris diangkat oleh RUPS berdasarkan kriteria yang ditetapkan dalam Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014 sebagai perikut.

1. Mempunyai akhlak, moral, dan integritas yang baik.  
2. Cakap makukan perbuatan hukum.  
3. Dalam 5 tahun sebelum pengangkatan dan selema menjabat:

a. Pernah tidak menyelenggarakan RUPS Tahunan;

b. Pertanggungjawabanya sebagai anggota Direksi dan/atau Dewan Komisaris pernah tidak diterima oleh RUPS kepada pernah tidak memberikan pertanggungjawaban sebagai anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris kepada RUPS; dan  
c. Pernah说我debabkan perusahaan yang memperoleh izin, persetujuan, atas pendaftaran dari Otoritas Jasa Keuangan tidak memenuhi kewajiban说我mpaikan Laporan Tahunan dan/atau Laporan Keuangan kepada Otoritas Jasa Keuangan.

4. Memiliki komitmen untuk mematuhi peraturan perundang-undangan.  
5. Memiliki pengetahunan dan/atau keahlian di bidang yang dibutuhkan Perseroan.

# Komposisi dan Masa Jabatan

Tidak terjadi perubahan dalam komposisi anggota Dewan Komisaris Selama tahun 2024, yang terdiri dari 1 Komisaris Utama dan 1 Komisaris Independen. Adapun,masa jabatan anggota Dewan Komisaris ditetapkan selama 5 tahun,sebagaimana disahkan dalam pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan.Namun,hal ini tidak mengurangi hak Pemegang Saham untuk memberhentikan anggota Dewan Komisaris sebelum masa jabatnya berakhir,berdasarkan atas yang dapat dipertanggungjawabkan.

The Board of Commissioners plays a role in carrying out supervisory functions and giving advice, suggestions, and recommendations to the Board of Directors regarding the management and administration of the Company as a whole.

# Work Guidelines

The working guidelines of the Board of Commissioners refer to the Articles of Association and Regulations of the Financial Services Authority No. 33/POJK.04/2014 about the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Criteria

The Board of Commissioners is appointed by the GMS based on the criteria set out in the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 33/POJK.04/2014 as follows.

1. Possesses good morals, ethics, and integrity.  
2. Capable of performing legal actions.  
3. In the 5 years prior to the appointment and during the tenure:

a. Has not failed to hold an Annual General Meeting of Shareholders (AGMS);  
b. Has had their accountability as a member of the Board of Directors and/or Board of Commissioners rejected by the AGMS or has failed to provide accountability as a member of the Board of Directors and/or Board of Commissioners to the AGMS; and  
c. Has caused a company that obtained a license, approval, or registration from the Financial Services Authority to fail to fulfill the obligation to submit the Annual Report and/or Financial Statements to the Financial Services Authority.

4. Committed to complying with laws and regulations.  
5. Possesses knowledge and/or expertise in the fields required by the Company.

# Composition and Term of Office

There is no change in the composition of the members of the Board of Commissioners during 2024, which consists of 1 President Commissioner and 1 Independent Commissioner. Meanwhile, the term of office of the members of the Board of Commissioners is set for 5 years, as authorized in the implementation of the Annual General Meeting of Shareholders. However, this does not reduce the right of Shareholders to dismiss members of the Board of Commissioners before their term of office ends, based on reasons that can be accounted for.

# Komisaris Independen

Komisaris Independenden Perseroan makeshift dijabat oleh Bapak Hadi Avilla Tamzil untuk periode jabatan 5 tahun ke depan. Pengangkatan beliau telah memenuhi ketentuan dalam Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014tentang Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Perusahaan Publik atau Emiten,{serta memenuhi kriteria sebagai Komisaris Independenden seksagai berikut.

1. Berasal dari luar perusahaan publik.  
2. Tidak mempunyai hubungan afliasi dengan Perseroan, Dewan Komisaris, Direksi dan/atau Pemegang Saham Utama perusahaan.  
3. Tidak memiliki hubungan usaha, baik langsung maupun tidak langsung, berkaitan dengan usaha Perseroan.  
4. Tidak memiliki saham, baik langsung maupun tidak langsung di Perseroan.  
5. Tidak bekerja rangkap sebagai Direktur di perusahaan lainnya yang terafiliasi dengan Perseroan.  
6. Dapat memahami peraturan perundang-undangan di bidang pasar modal.

# Independensi [IDX-G.01]

Seluruh anggota Dewan Komisaris berpegang seguh pada prinsip independensi, integritas, dan objektivitas dalam menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab mereka. Komitmen untuk menjaga kualitas pengawasan dan pengambilan keputusan yang adil dan transparan diwujudkan dengan tidak adanya hubungan afliliasi financial atop kekeluargaan antar pihak-pihak terkait. Hal ini memastikan oleh setiap keputusan yang diambil didasari oleh pertimbangan yang murni demi kepada perusahaan dan pemangku kepada tingtingan, ada mendukung dapat prinsip-prinsip GCG yang berlaku.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Berikut uraian(OP) mengenai tugas dan tanggung jawab Dewan Komisaris.

a. Melakukan pengawasan dan bertanggungjawab atas pengawasan terhadap kebijakan pengurusan, jalanya pengurusan pada umumnya, baik mengenai Perseroan maupun usaha Perseroan, dan memberi nasihat kepada Direksi.  
b. Memberikan persetujuan atas Rencana Kerja Tahunan Perseroan, selambat-lambatnya sebelum dimulainya tahun buku yang akan datang.  
c. Melakukan tugas yang secara khusus diberikan kepadaanya menurut Anggaran Dasar, peraturan perundang-undangan yang berlaku dan/atau berdasarkan keputusan RUPS.  
d. Melakukan tugas, wewenang, dan tanggung jawab seksuai dengan ketentuan Anggaran Dasar Perseroan dan keputusan RUPS.  
e. Meneliti dan menelaah Laporan Tahunan yang dispersiapkan oleh Direksianya menandatangani Laporan Tahunan tersebut.  
f. Mematuhi Anggaran Dasar dan peraturan perundangundangan, serta wajib melaksanakan prinsip-prinsepromesime, efisiensi, transparansi, kemandirian, akuntabilitas, pertanggungjawaban, serta kewajaran.

# Independent Commissioner

The Independent Commissioner of the Company is still held by Mr. Hadi Avilla Tamzil for the next 5-year term. His appointment complies with the provisions of the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 33/POJK.04/2014 on the Board of Commissioners and Directors of Public Companies or Issuers, and meets the criteria for an Independent Commissioner as follows.

1. Comes from outside the public company.  
2. Does not have any affiliation with the Company, the Board of Commissioners, the Board of Directors, and/or the Company's Majority Shareholders.  
3. Does not have any business relationship, either directly or indirectly, related to the Company's business.  
4. Does not own shares, either directly or indirectly, in the Company.  
5. Does not hold another directorship in a company affiliated with the Company.  
6. Capable of understanding laws and regulations in the capital market sector.

# Independency

All members of the Board of Commissioners adhere to the principles of independence, integrity, and objectivity in carrying out their duties and responsibilities. The commitment to maintain the quality of supervision and fair and transparent decision making is realized in the absence of a financial affiliation or family relationship between related parties. This ensures that every decision taken is based on purely for the benefit of the company and stakeholders, as well as supporting the implementation of the applicable GCG principles.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The following is an explanation of the duties and responsibilities of the Board of Commissioners.

a. supervise and be responsible for supervising management policies, the general management of both the Company and the Company's business, and provide advice to the Board of Directors.  
b. Give approval for the Company's Annual Work Plan, not later than before the start of the next financial year.  
c. Carry out tasks specifically assigned to him according to the Articles of Association, applicable laws and regulations and/or based on GMS decisions.  
d. Carry out duties, authorities and responsibilities in accordance with the provisions of the Company's Articles of Association and the resolutions of the GMS.  
e. Research and review the Annual Report prepared by the Board of Directors and sign the Annual Report.  
f. Comply with the Articles of Association and laws and regulations, and must implement the principles of professionalism, efficiency, transparency, independence, accountability, responsibility and fairness.

g. Melaksanakan fungsi nominasi dan remunerasi sesuai dengan ketentuan dan peraturan perundangundangan yang berlaku.  
h. Mengawasi pelaksanaan Rencana Kerja Tahunan Perseroan.  
i. Mengikuti perkembangan kegiatan Perseroan, dan dalam hal Perseroan menunjukkan gejala kemunduran yang mencolok, segera melaporkan kepada RUPS dengan disertai saran mengenai langkah perbaikan yang harus ditempuh.  
j. Memberikan pendapat dan saran kepada RUPS mengenai setiap persoalan lainnya yang dianggap penting bagi pengelolaan Perseroan.  
k. Melakukan tugas pengawasan lainnya yang ditentukan oleh RUPS.  
I. Memberikan tanggapan atas laporan berkala Direksi dan pada setiap waktu yang diperlukan mengenai perkembangan Perseroan

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab Komisaris Utama [Criteria PUGKI]

Komisaris Utama memiliki hak dan wewenang untuk memberikan arahan kepada anggota Dewan Komisaris, memimpinRAPAT internal maupun rapat gabungan antara Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi, serta memimpin pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan atas RUPS Luar Biasa.

# Keputusan yang Memerlukan Persetujuan Dewan Komisaris [Criteria PUGKI]

Dewan Komisaris mempunyai kewenangan tertentu dalam pengambilan keputusan strategis, termasuk di antaranya persetujuan atas pemindahan kepada penggunaan kekayaan Perseroan sebagai jaminan utang, persekituan untuk melakukan transaksi peminjaman kepada pemberian pinjaman, serta persetujuan untuk pendirian usaha tersebut participasi dalam perusahaan lain. Keputusan keputusan ini diambil untuk memastikan langkah-langkah yang diambil sejalan dengan kepentingan dan tujuan jangka panjang Perseroan.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Selama tahun 2024, Dewan Komisaris telah menjalankan tugas, tanggung jawab,{serta perannya dengan objektif dan profesional, yang dipaparkan sebagai berikut.

1. Mengawasi pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab Direksi secara keseluruhan.  
2. Memberikan saran, nasihat, serta rekomendasi sesuai dengan kebjakan dan strategi yang dibutuhkan oleh Direksi.  
3. Menyampaikan Laporan Pengawasan Dewan Komisaris dalam RUPS Tahunan.  
4. Melakukan rapat internal Dewan Komisaris sebanyak 6 kali, serta rapat gabungan bersama Direksi sebanyak 6 kali pada tahun 2024.  
5. Melakukan rapat gabungan dengan Komite Audit.  
6. Melakukan evaluasi atas audit Laporan Keuangan yang dilakukan oleh kantor akuntan publik tahun buku 2023 dan menuunjuk akuntan publik/kantor akuntan publik atas rekomendasi Komite Audit.

g. Carry out the nomination and remuneration functions in accordance with the applicable laws and regulations.  
h. Supervise the implementation of the Company's Annual Work Plan.  
i. Following the development of the Company's activities, and in the event that the Company shows striking symptoms of decline, immediately report to the GMS accompanied by suggestions regarding corrective steps that must be taken.  
j. Provide opinions and suggestions to the GMS regarding any other issues deemed important for the management of the Company.  
k. Carry out other supervisory duties determined by the GMS.  
I. Provide responses to the periodic reports of the Board of Directors and at any time necessary regarding the development of the Company.

# Duties and Responsibilities of President Commissioner

The President Commissioner has the right and authority to provide guidance to the members of the Board of Commissioners, lead internal meetings as well as joint meetings between the Board of Commissioners and the Board of Directors, and oversee the implementation of the Annual GMS or Extraordinary GMS.

# Decisions Requiring Board of Commissioners Approval

The Board of Commissioners has certain authority in making strategic decisions, including approval of the transfer or use of the Company's assets as collateral for debt, approval of loan or lending transactions, as well as approval for establishing new businesses or participating in other companies. These decisions are made to ensure that the steps taken align with the Company's interests and long-term objectives.

# Implementation of Tasks

During 2024, the Board of Commissioners has carried out its duties, responsibilities, and roles with objectivity and professionalism, as outlined below.

1. Supervise the implementation of duties and responsibilities of the Board of Directors as a whole.  
2. Provide advice, advice, and recommendations in accordance with policies and strategies required by the Board of Directors.  
3. Submit the Supervisory Report of the Board of Commissioners at the Annual GMS.  
4. Conducting internal meetings of the Board of Commissioners as many as 6 times, as well as joint meetings with the Board of Directors as many as 6 times in 2024.  
5. Conduct joint meetings with the Audit Committee.  
6. Evaluate the Financial Statement audit conducted by a public accounting firm for the 2023 financial year and appoint a public accountant/public accounting firm on the recommendation of the Audit Committee.

# Rapat [IDX-G.02]

Rapat internal Dewan Komisaris diadakan minimal sekali setiap 3 bulan, dan rapat gabungan dengan Direksi minimal sekali setiap 4 bulan. Pada tahun 2024, Dewan Komisaris telah mengadakan rapat internal sebanyak 6 kali dan rapat gabungan dengan Direksi sebanyak 6 kali, sebagai berikut.

# Meeting

The internal meeting of the Board of Commissioners is held at least once every 3 months, and a joint meeting with the Board of Directors at least once every 4 months. In 2024, the Board of Commissioners has held internal meetings 6 times and joint meetings with the Board of Directors 6 times, as follows.

# Pengembangan Kompetensi [IDX-G.05]

Perseroan memberikan kesempatan penuh kepada anggota Dewan Komisaris untukCCCCCC terbagai kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi, baik yang diselenggarakan oleh pihak internal, pihak ketiga, maupun melalui media online dan offline secara mandiri. Selama tahun 2024, kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi yang diikuti oleh Dewan Komisaris dijabarkan sebagai berikut.

# Competency Development

The Company gives full opportunities to members of the Board of Commissioners to participate in various competency development activities, both organized by internal parties, third parties, or through online and offline media independently. During 2024, the competency development activities participated by the Board of Commissioners are described as follows.

# Penilaian Kinerja Dewan Komisaris dan Komite Pendukung

# Penilaian Kinerja Dewan Komisaris [IDX-G.04]

# Prosedur Penilaian Kinerja

Penilaian kinerja Dewan Komisaris dilakukan oleh Pemegang Saham dalam RUPS Tahunan melalui penyampaian Laporan Pengawasan. Selain itu, setup anggota Dewan Komisaris juga makukan penilaian diri (self-assessment) berdasarkan kriteria yang telah disepadakit.

# Performance Assessment of the Board of Commissioners and Supporting Committees

# Performance Assessment of the Board of Commissioners

# Performance Assessment Procedure

The performance assessment of the Board of Commissioners is carried out by the Shareholders in the Annual GMS through the submission of the Supervisory Report. In addition, each member of the Board of Commissioners also conducts a self-assessment based on the criteria that have been agreed upon.

# Kriteria Penilaian Kinerja

Perseroan telah menetapkan kriteria penilaian Dewan Komisaris yang terdiri dari pelaksanaan rapat internal dan rapat gabungan dengan Direksi, tingkat kehadiran dan participasi dalam rapat, kontribusi dalam pengawasan, seda kualitas dan intensitas pemberian saran kepada Direksi.

# Hasil Penilaian

Dewan Komisaris telah melaksananakahugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik dan profesional selama tahun 2024. Selain itu, saran, nasihat, dan rekomendasi yang diberikan telah memberikan dampak positif terhadap kinerja Perseroan secara keseluruhan.

# Penilaian Kinerja Komite Pendukung

# Prosedur Penilaian Kinerja

Dewan Komisaris secara berkala seksukan penilaian kinerja kepada Komite Audit{serta Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi. Penilaian tersebut bertujuan untuk mencevausi kinerja, pencapaian target, dan memberikan rekomendasi atas aspek-aspek kerja yang belum diterapkan secara optimal.

# Kriteria Penilaian Kinerja

Kriteria penilaian kinerja komite pendukung Dewan Komisaris terdiri dari efektivitas dalam menjalankan tugas, kehadiran dan participasi aktif dalam rapat,{serta kualitas rekomendasi dan saran yang disampaikan kepada Dewan Komisaris.

# Hasil Penilaian

Pada tahun 2024, Dewan Komisaris menjadi Komite Audit seda Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi telah melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik, objektif, dan sesuai dengan kebjikan yang berlaku.

Direksi bertanggung jawab atas pengelolaan operasional dan keuangan Perseroan untuk mencapai Visi, Misi, dan target yang ditetapkan, dengan tetap mematuhi prinsip kehati-hatian dan kepadahan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Pedoman kerja Direksi merujuk pada Anggaran Dasar dan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014tentang Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Emiten atas Perusahaan Publik.

# Criteria [IDX-G.06]

Direksi diangkat oleh RUPS berdasarkan kriteria yang ditetapkan dalam Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014 sebagai perikut.

1. Mempunyai akhlak, moral, dan integritas yang baik.  
2. Cakap melakukan perbuatan hukum.

# Performance Assessment Criteria

The Company has established evaluation criteria for the Board of Commissioners, which include the implementation of internal meetings and joint meetings with the Board of Directors, attendance and participation levels in meetings, contributions to supervision, as well as the quality and intensity of providing advice to the Board of Directors.

# Assessment Results

The Board of Commissioners has carried out its duties and responsibilities effectively and professionally throughout 2024. Furthermore, the advice, counsel, and recommendations provided have had a positive impact on the overall performance of the Company.

# Performance Assessment of the Supporting Committees

# Performance Assessment Procedure

The Board of Commissioners periodically conducts performance assessments of the Audit Committee and the Nomination and Remuneration Committee. The assessment aims to evaluate performance, target achievement, and provide recommendations on aspects of work that have not been optimally implemented.

# Performance Assessment Criteria

The criteria for assessing the performance of the supporting committees of the Board of Commissioners include the effectiveness in carrying out tasks, attendance and active participation in meetings, as well as the quality of recommendations and advice provided to the Board of Commissioners.

# Assessment Results

In 2024, the Board of Commissioners assessed that the Audit Committee and the Nomination and Remuneration Committee had carried out their duties and responsibilities effectively, objectively, and in accordance with applicable policies.

# DIREKSI

# BOARD OF DIRECTORS

The Board of Directors is responsible for the Company's operational and financial management to achieve the Vision, Mission, and set targets, while still complying with the principles of caution and compliance.

# Work Guidelines

The working guidelines of the Board of Directors refer to the Articles of Association and the Regulation of the Financial Services Authority No. 33/POJK.04/2014 about the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Criteria

The Board of Directors is appointed by the GMS based on the criteria set out in the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 33/POJK.04/2014 as follows.

1. Possesses good morals, ethics, and integrity.  
2. Capable of performing legal actions.

3. Dalam 5 tahun sebelum pengangkatan dan selema menjabat:  
a. Pernah tidak menyelenggarakan RUPS Tahunan;  
b. Pertanggungjawabanya sebagai anggota Direksi dan/atau Dewan Komisaris pernah tidak diterima oleh RUPS kepada pernah tidak memberikan pertanggungjawaban sebagai anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris kepada RUPS; dan  
c. Pernah menyebabkan perusahaan yang memperoleh izin, persetujuan, atas pendaftaran dari Otoritas Jasa Keuangan tidak memenuhi kewajiban mencampaikan Laporan Tahunan dan/atau Laporan Keuangan kepada Otoritas Jasa Keuangan.  
4. Memiliki komitmen untuk mematuhi peraturan perundang-undangan.  
5. Memiliki pengetahuan dan/atau keahlian di bidang yang dibutuhkan Perseroan.

# Komposisi dan Masa Jabatan

Tidak terjadi perubahan dalam komposisi anggota Direksi selama tahun 2024, yang terdiri dari 1 Direktur Utama dan 3 Direktur. Adapun,ASA jabatan anggota Direksi ditetapkan selama 5 tahun, sebagai disahkan dalam pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan. Namun, hal ini tidak mengurangi hak Pemegang Saham untuk memberhentikan anggota Direksi sebelummasa jabatanya berakhir, berdasarkan alasan yang dapat dipertanggungjawabkan.

3. In the 5 years prior to the appointment and during the tenure:  
a. Has not failed to hold an Annual General Meeting of Shareholders (AGMS);  
b. Has had their accountability as a member of the Board of Directors and/or Board of Commissioners rejected by the AGMS or has failed to provide accountability as a member of the Board of Directors and/or Board of Commissioners to the AGMS; and  
c. Has caused a company that obtained a license, approval, or registration from the Financial Services Authority to fail to fulfill the obligation to submit the Annual Report and/or Financial Statements to the Financial Services Authority.  
4. Committed to complying with laws and regulations.  
5. Possesses knowledge and/or expertise in the fields required by the Company.

# Composition and Term of Office

There was no change in the composition of the Board of Directors during 2024, which consisted of 1 President Director and 3 Directors. Meanwhile, the term of office of the Board of Directors is set for 5 years, as authorized in the implementation of the Annual General Meeting of Shareholders. However, this does not reduce the right of Shareholders to dismiss members of the Board of Directors before their term of office ends, based on accountable reasons.

# Tugas, Tanggung Jawab, dan Wewenang

# Tugas

a. Direksi bertugas menjalankan dan bertanggung jawab atas pengurusan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik untuk kepentingan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik yang ditetapkan dalam Anggaran Dasar.

# Duties, Responsibilities, and Authority

# Duties

a. The Board of Directors is responsible for managing and overseeing the operations of the Issuer or Public Company in the best interest of the Issuer or Public Company, in accordance with the objectives set out in the Articles of Association.

b. Dalam menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab atas pengurusan sebagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (1), Direksi wajib说我yelenggarakan RUPS Tahunan dan RUPS lainnya sebagaimana diatur dalam peraturan perdang-undangan dan Anggaran Dasar.  
c. Setiap anggota Direksi wajib melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab sebagaiimana dimaksud pada ayat (1) dengan itikad baik, penuh tanggung jawab, dan kehati-hatian.  
d. Dalam rangka mendukung efektivitas pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab sebagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (1) Direksi dapat membentuk komite.  
e. Dalam hal dibentuk komite seksagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (4), Direksi wajib melakukan evaluasi terhadap kinerja komite setiap akhir tahun buku.

# Tanggung Jawab

a. Setiap anggota Direksi bertanggung jawab secara tinggung renteng atas kerugian Emiten oleh Perusahaan Publik yang disebabkan oleh kesalahan oleh kelalaian anggota Direksi dalam menjalankan tugasnya.  
b. Anggota Direksi tidak dapat dipertanggungjawabkan atas kerugian Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik sebagai dimaksud pada ayat (1) apabila dapat membuktikan:

- Kerugian tersebut bukan karena kesalahan ata kalalaiannya;  
- Telah melakukan pengurusan dengan itikad baik, penuh tanggung jawab, dan kehati-hatian untuk kepentingan dan sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik;  
- Tidak mempunyai benturan kepentingan baik langsung maupun tidak langsung atas tindakan pengurusan yang mengakibatkan kerugian; dan  
- Telah mencambil tindakan untuk mencegah timbul kepada berlanjutnya kerugian tersebut.

Selain melaksanakan tugas secara kolektif, Direksi juga memiliki pembagian tugas yang seksu dengan jabatan masing-masing untuk mengoptimalkan pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab mereka.

b. In carrying out the duties and responsibilities of management as referred to in paragraph (1), the Board of Directors must hold the Annual GMS and other GMS as regulated by the laws and the Articles of Association.  
c. Each member of the Board of Directors must carry out their duties and responsibilities as referred to in paragraph (1) with good faith, full responsibility, and due diligence.  
d. To support the effective implementation of their duties and responsibilities as referred to in paragraph (1), the Board of Directors may establish committees.  
e. If committees are established as referred to in paragraph (4), the Board of Directors must evaluate the performance of the committees at the end of each fiscal year.

# Responsibilities

a. Each member of the Board of Directors is jointly and severally responsible for the losses of the Issuer or Public Company caused by errors or negligence on the part of the Board members in performing their duties.  
b. A member of the Board of Directors cannot be held accountable for the losses of the Issuer or Public Company as referred to in paragraph (1) if they can prove:

- The loss was not due to their error or negligence;  
- They have acted in good faith, with full responsibility, and due diligence for the benefit and in accordance with the objectives of the Issuer or Public Company;  
- They have no conflict of interest, either directly or indirectly, regarding the management actions that resulted in the loss; and  
- They have taken action to prevent the occurrence or continuation of the loss.

In addition to performing their duties collectively, the Board of Directors also has task allocations according to their respective positions to optimize the execution of their duties and responsibilities.

# Wewenang

1. Direksi berwenang menjalankan pengurusan sebagai dimaksud dalam Pasal 12 sesuai dengan kebjikan yang dipandang kepada, sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan yang ditetapkan dalam Anggaran Dasar.  
2. Direksi berwenang mewakili Emiten atas Perusahaan Publik di dalam dan di luar pengadilan.  
3. Anggota Direksi tidak berwenang mewakili Emiten希望大家 Perusahaan Publik apabila:

a. Terdapat perkara di pengadilan antara Emiten atau Perusahaan Publik dengan anggota Direksi yang bersangkutan; dan  
b. Anggota Direksi yang bersangkutan mempunyai kepentinganyang berbenturan dengan kepentingan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik.

4. Dalam hal terdapat keadaan seksagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (2), yang berhak mewakili Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik adalah:

a. Anggota Direksi lainnya yang tidak mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik;  
b. Dewan Komisaris dalam hal seluruh anggota Direksi mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik; oleh  
c. Pihak lain yang ditunjuk oleh RUPS dalam hal seluruh anggota Direksi untuk Dewan Komisaris mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik.

# Authorities

1. The Board of Directors is authorized to manage the affairs as outlined in Article 12 in accordance with policies deemed appropriate, in line with the aims and objectives set forth in the Articles of Association.  
2. The Board of Directors is authorized to represent the Issuer or Public Company both in and outside of court.  
3. A member of the Board of Directors is not authorized to represent the Issuer or Public Company if:

a. There is a legal case between the Issuer or Public Company and the concerned member of the Board of Directors; or  
b. The concerned member of the Board of Directors has a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company.

4. In the event of the situations described in paragraph (2), the party authorized to represent the Issuer or Public Company is:

a. Another member of the Board of Directors who does not have a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company;  
b. The Board of Commissioners if all members of the Board of Directors have a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company; or  
c. A third party appointed by the General Meeting of Shareholders if all members of the Board of Directors or the Board of Commissioners have a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Selama tahun 2024, Direksi telah melaksanakan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya dengan baik dan profesional, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Melaporkan pengelolaan dan pengurusan Perseroan kepada Pemegang Saham di dalam pelaksanaan RUPS.  
2. Melaksanakan RUPS Tahunan dan RUPS Luar Biasa, sama Paparan Publik pada tanggal 5 Juni 2024.  
3. Melakukan penyusunan kebijakan dan strategi bisnis Perseroan, termasuk rencana jangka pendek,(OP) mengah,dan panjang.  
4. Melakukan evaluasi kinerja organ pendukung, yaitu Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal.  
5. Mengikuti rapat gabungan bersama Dewan Komisaris atau dengan Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal.

# Rapat [IDX-G.02]

Direksi melaksanan rapat internal minimal sekali setiap bulan, dan rapat gabungan dengan Dewan Komisaris minimal sekali setiap 3 bulan. Pada tahun 2024, Direksi telah melaksanan rapat internal sebanyak 20 kali dan rapat gabungan sebanyak 6 kali, yang dijelaskan sebagai berikut.

# Implementation of Duties

During 2024, the Board of Directors has carried out its duties and responsibilities well and professionally, as outlined below.

1. Reporting the management and administration of the Company to the Shareholders during the implementation of the GMS.  
2. Holding the Annual GMS and Extraordinary GMS, and Public Expose on June 5, 2024.  
3. Formulating the Company's business policies and strategies, including short-term, medium-term, and long-term plans.  
4. Conducting performance evaluations of supporting organs, namely the Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit.  
5. Attending joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners or with the Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit.

# Meeting

The Board of Directors conducts internal meetings at least once a month, and joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners at least once every 3 months. In 2024, the Board of Directors has held internal meetings as many as 20 times and joint meetings as many as 6 times, which is explained as follows.

# Pengembangan Kompetensi [IDX-G.05]

Perseroan memberikan kesempatan penuh kepada anggota Direksi untuk mengikuti berbagai kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi, baik yang diselenggarakan oleh pihak internal, pihak ketiga, maupun melalui media online dan offline secara mandiri. Selama tahun 2024, kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi yang diikuti oleh Direksi dibabarkan sebagai berikut.

# Competency Development

The Company gives full opportunities to members of the Board of Directors to participate in various competency development activities, both held by internal parties, third parties, and through online and offline media independently. During 2024, the competency development activities followed by the Board of Directors are described as follows.

<table><tr><td>Topik
Topic</td><td>Penyelenggara

# Penilaian Kinerja Direksi dan Organ Pendukung Direksi

# Penilaian Kinerja Direksi [IDX-G.04]

# Prosedur Penilaian Kinerja

Penilaian kinerja Direksi dilakukan oleh Pemegang Saham dalam RUPS Tahunan melalui penyampaian Laporan Pengelolaan dan Pengurusan Perseroan. Selain itu, setiap anggota Direksi juga makukan penilaian diri (self-assessment) berdasarkan kriteria yang telah disepadaki.

# Kriteria Penilaian Kinerja

Perseroan telah menetapkan kriteria penilaian Direksi yang terdiri dari pelaksanaan rapat internal dan rapat gabungan dengan Dewan Komisaris, tingkat kehadiran dan participasi dalam rapat, penetapan kebujakan dan strategi, serta kualitas dan intensitas pemberian saran kepada Direksi.

# Hasil Penilaian

Pada tahun 2024, Direksi telah menjalankanugas, tanggung jawab,{serta wewenangnya dengan objektif, profesional,dan sesuai dengan ketentuan yang berlaku.

# Performance Evaluation of the Board of Directors and Supporting Organs of the Board of Directors

# Performance Appraisal of Board of Directors

# Performance Assessment Procedure

The performance of the Board of Directors is assessed by the Shareholders at the Annual General Meeting (AGM) through the submission of the Company's Management and Administration Report. Additionally, each member of the Board of Directors conducts a self-assessment based on the criteria that have been agreed upon.

# Performance Assessment Criteria

The Company has established performance evaluation criteria for the Board of Directors, which include the execution of internal meetings and joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners, attendance and participation in meetings, policy and strategy formulation, as well as the quality and intensity of recommendations provided to the Board of Directors.

# Assessment Results

In 2024, the Board of Directors has carried out its duties, responsibilities, and authority objectively, professionally, and in accordance with applicable regulations.

# Penilaian Organ Pendukung Direksi

# Prosedur Penilaian Kinerja

Direksi secara Berkala melakukan penilaian kinerja kepada Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal. Penilaian tersebut bertujuan untuk mengevaluasi kinerja, mencapaian target, dan memberikan rekomendasi atas aspek-aspek kerja yang belum diterapkan secara optimal.

# Kriteria Penilaian Kinerja

Kriteria penilaian kinerja organ pendukung Direksi terdiri dari efektivitas pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab, tingkat kehadiran dan keaktifan dalam rapat, pencapaian target, serta kualitas rekomendasi dan saran yang diberikan kepada Direksi.

# Hasil Penilaian

Direksi menjadi Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal telah menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya dengan efektif selama tahun 2024.

# Komite di Bawah Direksi

Direksi tidak mementuk komite di bawah Direksi, oleh karena itu informasi tersebut tidak terdapat dalam Laporan Tahunan ini.

# Assessment of Supporting Organs of the Board of Directors

# Performance Assessment Procedure

The Board of Directors periodically conducts performance evaluations of the Corporate Secretary and the Internal Audit Unit. The purpose of these evaluations is to assess performance, target achievement, and provide recommendations for areas of work that have not been optimally implemented.

# Performance Assessment Criteria

The performance evaluation criteria for the supporting organs of the Board of Directors include the effectiveness in carrying out duties and responsibilities, attendance and participation levels in meetings, achievement of targets, and the quality of recommendations and advice provided to the Board of Directors.

# Assessment Results

The Board of Directors assesses that the Corporate Secretary and the Internal Audit Unit have carried out their duties and responsibilities effectively throughout 2024.

# Committee Under the Board of Directors

The Board of Directors has not established any committees under the Board of Directors, therefore, this information is not included in this Annual Report.

# ASPEK PENTING TERKAIT DEWAN KOMISARIS DAN DIREKSI

# IMPORTANT ASPECTS RELATED TO THE BOARD OF COMMISSIONERS AND BOARD OF DIRECTORS

# Kebijakan Remunerasi dan Nominasi

# Kebijakan Remunerasi

# Prosedur

Remunerasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi ditetapkan oleh Pemegang Saham dalam RUPS Tahunan, dengan memperhatikan ketentuan Anggaran Dasar, kebanyak terkait, serta rekomendasi dari Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi. Kenaikan remunerasi, jika ada, tidak melebihi  $10\%$  dari jujiah remunerasi yang ditetapkan pada tahun sebelumnya.

# Dasar Penetapan Remunerasi

Penetapan remunerasi juga memperhatikan kondisi internal perusahaan, serta situasi ekonomi dan industri terkini. Selain itu, Perseroan juga mempertimbangkan berbagai aspek berikut.

1. Remunerasi yang berlaku pada industri sesuai dengan kegiatan usaha Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik sejenis dan skala usaha dari Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik dalam industrinya.  
2. Tugas, tanggung jawab, dan wewenang anggota Dewan Komisaris dan/atau Direksi dikaitkan dengan pencapaian tujuan dan kinerja Emiten atau Perusahaan Publik.  
3. Target kinerja atau kinerja masing - masing anggota Dewan Komisaris dan/atau anggota Direksi.  
4. Keseimbangan tunjangan antara yang bersifat tetap dan bersifat variabel.

# Remuneration and Nomination Policy

# Remuneration Policy

# Procedure

The remuneration of the Board of Commissioners and the Board of Directors is determined by the Shareholders in the Annual GMS, taking into account the provisions of the Articles of Association, relevant policies, and recommendations from the Nomination and Remuneration Committee. Any increase in remuneration, if applicable, does not exceed  $10\%$  of the remuneration set in the previous year.

# Basis for Determining Remuneration

The determination of remuneration also takes into account the company's internal conditions, as well as the current economic and industry situation. Additionally, the company considers the following aspects.

1. The remuneration applicable in the industry according to the business activities of the issuer or similar public companies and the scale of the issuer or public company in its industry.  
2. The duties, responsibilities, and authority of the members of the Board of Commissioners and/or Board of Directors are linked to the achievement of the goals and performance of the issuer or public company.  
3. The performance targets or achievements of each member of the Board of Commissioners and/or Board of Directors.  
4. The balance between fixed and variable allowances.

# Struktur Remunerasi

Struktur remunerasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Perseroan terdiri dari gaji dan tunjangan lainnya.

# Besaran Remunerasi

Pada tahun 2024, Perseroan telah membayarkan remunerasi kepada Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi sebesar Rp525 juta, menc Gat dibandingkan tahun sebelumnya yang tercatat sebesar Rp492 juta.

# Kebijakan Nominasi

Perseroan telah menetapkan kebijakan nominasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi mengusulkanNama calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi kepada Pemegang Saham dan Direksi.  
2. Apabila name-name yang diusulkan telah disetujui,.make Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi berwenang memanggil calon tersebut untuk makukutan prosedur pemilihan dan berbagai的前提下 lainnya, termasuk wawancara jika dibutuhkan. Calon-calon terpilih merupakan calon yang memenuhi kriteria Perseroan.  
3. Calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan anggota Direksi yang terpilih harus tersebut uji kepada tan dan kelayakan.  
4. Calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan anggota Direksi yang terpilih disahkan dan ditetapkan dalam pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan.

# Pencegahan Konflik Kepentingan [IDX-G.09]

Untuk mencegah potensi konflik kepentingan, Perseroan mencapkan kebijakan yang mengharuskan anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi untuk mengungkapkan setiap kepentingan pribadi yang dapat mempengaruhi objektivitas dan keputusan perusahaan. Mereka juga diwajibkan untuk mematuhi Kode Etik dan pedoman perilaku yang menginepankan transparansi seda integritas dalam setiap tindakan dan keputusan yang diambil. Selain itu, Komite Audit Perseroan memiligi kewenangan untuk mengawasi dan menindaklanjuti apabila terjadi konflik kepentingan antara organ utama, guna memastikan bahwa setiap keputusan yang diambil tetap berfokus pada kepentingan terbaik perusahaan dan Pemegang Saham.

# Remuneration Structure

The remuneration structure for the Board of Commissioners and the Board of Directors of the Company consists of salary and other allowances.

# Remuneration Amount

In 2024, the Company paid a total remuneration of Rp525 million to the Board of Commissioners and the Board of Directors, an increase compared to the previous year's amount of Rp492 million.

# Nomination Policy

The company has established a nomination policy for the Board of Commissioners and Directors, which is outlined as follows.

1. The Nomination and Remuneration Committee proposes the names of prospective members of the Board of Commissioners and Directors to the Shareholders and Board of Directors.  
2. If the proposed names have been approved, the Nomination and Remuneration Committee has the authority to summon the candidate to conduct selection procedures and various other stages, including interviews if needed. The selected candidates are candidates who meet the Company's criteria.  
3. Candidates for members of the Board of Commissioners and elected members of the Board of Directors must take the appropriateness and feasibility test.  
4. Candidates for members of the Board of Commissioners and elected members of the Board of Directors are ratified and determined in the implementation of the Annual GMS.

# Prevention of Conflict of Interest

To prevent potential conflicts of interest, the Company implements a policy that requires members of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors to disclose any personal interests that can affect the objectivity and company's decisions. They are also required to comply with the Code of Ethics and guidelines of conduct that prioritize transparency and integrity in every action and decision taken. In addition, the Company's Audit Committee has the authority to supervise and follow up in the event of a conflict of interest between the main organs, to ensure that every decision taken remains focused on the best interests of the company and Shareholders.

# Keberagaman Komposisi [IDX-G.01]

Perseroan telah memastikan adanya keberagaman dalam komposisi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi, yang mencakup berbagai latar belakang, pengalaman, keahlian, dan perspektif. Keberagaman ini bertujuan untuk mengefektifkan proses pengambilan keputusan, mencatkan inovasi, serta memperkuat pengawasan dan manajemen Perseroan. Selain itu, Perseroan dapat lebih responsif terhadap perubahanasar dan tantangan bisnis, serta mencerminkan komitmen Perseroan terhadap prinsip inklusivitas dan transparansi dalam pengelolaan perusahaan.

# Program Orientasi

Tidak terdapat perubahan dalam komposisi Dewan Komisaris maupun Direksi pada tahun 2024. Oleh karena itu, tidak dilaksanan program orientasi selamaperiode tersebut.

# Composition Diversity

The Company has ensured diversity in the composition of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors, which includes various backgrounds, experiences, expertise, and perspectives. This diversity aims to make the decision-making process more effective, increase innovation, and strengthen the supervision and management of the Company. In addition, the Company can be more responsive to market changes and business challenges, as well as reflect the Company's commitment to the principles of inclusivity and transparency in company management.

# Orientation Program

There were no changes in the composition of the Board of Commissioners or the Board of Directors in 2024. Therefore, no orientation program was conducted during this period.

# KOMITE AUDIT

# AUDIT COMMITTEE

Komite Audit dibentuk untuk mendukung pengawasan yang efektif oleh Dewan Komisaris, termasuk melaksanan audit Laporan Keuangan secara Berkala, memastikan;penerapan;(systempengendalian internal dan manajemen risiko,serta memantau pelaksanaan GCG);;(secaresenyluruh.

# Pedoman Kerja

Pedoman kerja Komite Audit merujuk pada Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 55/POJK.04/2015 tersebut Pembentukan dan Pedoman Pelaksanaan Kerja Komite Audit.

The Audit Committee was established to support effective supervision by the Board of Commissioners, including conducting periodic audits of Financial Statements, ensuring the implementation of internal control systems and risk management, and monitoring the implementation of GCG thoroughly.

# Composition and Membership

The Audit Committee's working guidelines refer to the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 55/POJK.04/2015 regarding the Establishment and Guidelines for the Implementation of Audit Committee Work.

# Komposisi dan Masa Jabatan

Sepanjang tahun 2024, tidak terdapat perubahan dalam kompositisi Komite Audit, yang terdiri dari 1 Ketua dan 2 anggota yang berasal dari pihak eksternal, sesuai dengan ketentuan yang berlaku. Masa jabatan anggota Komite Audit mengikutama jabatan Dewan Komisaris dan dapat diberhentikan sewaktu-waktu denganalan yang jelas.

# Composition and Term of Office

Throughout 2024, there is no change in the composition of the Audit Committee, which consists of 1 Chairman and 2 members from external parties, in accordance with the applicable provisions. The term of office of an Audit Committee member follows the term of office of the Board of Commissioners and can be dismissed at any time with clear reasons.

# Independensi

Komite Audit bergomitmen untuk bekerja secara independen tanpa intervensi dan menghindari benturan kepentingan, guna memastikan pengawasan yang efektif, transparan, dan mendukung tata kelola perusahaan yang baik. Komitmen ini tercermin melalui pemenuhan aspek independensi berikut.

# Independency

The Audit Committee is committed to working independently without intervention and avoiding conflicts of interest, in order to ensure effective, transparent supervision, and support good corporate governance. This commitment is reflected through the fulfillment of the following aspects of independence.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Berikut uraian(OP) mengenai tugas dan tanggung jawab Komite Audit.

1. Melakukan penelaahan atas informasi keuangan yang akan dikeluarkan Perseroan kepada publik dan/atau pihak otoritas, antara lain Laporan Keuangan, projeksi dan laporan lainnya terkait dengan informasi keuangan Perseroan, termasuk kepada terhadap standar dan kebikan akuntansi dalam proses penyusunannya.  
2. Melakukan penelaahan atas ketaatan terhadap peraturan perundang-undangan yang berhubungan dengan kegiatan Perseroan.  
3. Memberikan pendapat independen dalam hal terjadi perbedaan pendapat antara manajemen dan akuntan eksternal atas jasa yang diferikannya.  
4. Memberikan rekomendasi kepada Dewan Komisaris mengenai penunjukkan akuntan yang didasarkan pada independensi, ruang lingkup penugasan, dan imbalan jasa.  
5. Mendorong terbentuknya systemd pengendalian internal yang memadai dalam pengelolaan perusahaan dengan makukan evaluasi dan memberikan rekomendasi mengenai penyempurnaan systemd pengendalian internal perusahaan dan implementasinya.  
6. Melakukan penelaahan atas pelaksanaan pemeriksaan oleh auditor internal dan mengawasi pelaksanaan tindak lanjut oleh Direksi atas temuan auditor internal.  
7. Melakukan penelaahan terhadap aktivitas pelaksanaan systemd manajemen risiko yang dilakukan oleh Direksi.  
8. Menelaah pengaduan yang Berkaitan dengan proses akuntansi dan pelaporan keuangan Perseroan.  
9. Menelaah independensi dan objektivitas akuntan publik.  
10. Melakukan penelaahan atas kecukupan pemeriksuan yang dilakukan oleh akuntan publik.  
11. Melakukan pemeriksaan terhadap dugaan adanya kesalahan dalam keputusan rapat Direksi atau penyimpangan dalam pelaksanaan telah keputusan rapat Direksi.  
12. Menyampaikan laporan telah penelaahan kepada seluruh anggota Dewan Komisaris Perseroan setelah selesainya laporan telah penelaahan yang dilakukan oleh Komite Audit.  
13. Menelaah dan memberikan saran kepada Dewan Komisaris terkait adanya potensi benturan kepentingan Perseroan.  
14. Menjaga kerahasiaan dokumen, data, dan informasi Perseroan.  
15. Melaksanakan tugas lain dari Dewan Komisaris terkait dengan peran dan tanggung jawab Dewan Komisaris.

# Wewenang

Selain menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab, Komite Audit memiliki wewenang sebagai berikut.

1. Mengakses dokumen, data, dan informasi PerseroanARP tentang karyawan, dana, aset, dan sumber daya yang diperlukan.  
2. Berkomunikasi langsung dengan karyawan, termasuk Direksi dan pihak yang menjalankan fungsi audit internal, manajemen risiko, dan akuntan erkaitugas dan tanggung jawab Komite Audit.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The following is a description of the duties and responsibilities of the Audit Committee.

1. Reviewing the financial information that will be issued by the Company to the public and/or authorities, including financial reports, projections and other reports related to the Company's financial information, including compliance with accounting standards and policies in the preparation process.  
2. Review compliance with laws and regulations related to the Company's activities.

3. Provide an independent opinion in the event of a difference of opinion between the management and the external accountant for the services they provide.  
4. Provide recommendations to the Board of Commissioners regarding the appointment of an accountant based on independence, scope of assignment, and compensation for services.  
5. Encouraging the establishment of an adequate internal control system in managing the company by evaluating and providing recommendations regarding the improvement of the company's internal control system and its implementation.  
6. Reviewing the implementation of inspections by the internal auditors and overseeing the implementation of follow-up actions by the Board of Directors on the findings of the internal auditors.  
7. Reviewing the implementation of risk management system activities carried out by the Board of Directors.  
8. Examine complaints related to the Company's accounting and financial reporting processes.  
9. Examine the independence and objectivity of public accountants.  
10. Reviewing the adequacy of audits conducted by public accountants.  
11. Examine allegations of errors in the decisions of the Board of Directors meetings or irregularities in implementing the decisions of the Board of Directors meetings.  
12. Delivering the review report to all members of the Company's Board of Commissioners after the completion of the review report conducted by the Audit Committee.  
13. Review and provide advice to the Board of Commissioners regarding potential conflicts of interest of the Company.  
14. Maintain the confidentiality of the Company's documents, data, and information.  
15. Carry out other duties of the Board of Commissioners related to the roles and responsibilities of the Board of Commissioners.

# Authorities

In addition to carrying out its duties and responsibilities, the Audit Committee has the following authorities.

1. Accessing the Company's documents, data, and information related to employees, funds, assets, and resources required.  
2. Communicating directly with employees, including the Board of Directors and those carrying out internal audit functions, risk management, and accountants regarding the duties and responsibilities of the Audit Committee.

3. Melibatkan pihak independen di luar Komite Audit yang diperlukan untuk membantu pelaksanaan tugasnya (jika diperlukan).  
4. Melakukan kewenangan lain yang diberikan oleh Dewan Komisaris.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Komite Audit telah menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik dan efektif selama tahun 2024, yang dipaparkan sebagai berikut.

1. Melakukaan penelaahan terhadap Laporan Keuangan Triwulanan dan Tahunan Perseroan.  
2. Melakukan pengawasan terhadap systemd pengendalian internal dan manajemen risiko.  
3. Melakukan penelaahan terhadap temuan dari Unit Audit Internal, ada memantau tindak lanjut rekomendasi atas temuan audit tersebut.  
4. Menyusun dan menuyampaikan laporan tersebut dan rekomendasi kepada Komisaris utama.  
5. Melakukan pengawasan menyeluruh terhadap;penerapan GCG, termasuk mengawai potensi-potensi benturan kepentingan antara organ perusahaan.

# Rapat

Komite Audit menjadi rapat internal setidaknya sekali setup 3 bulan atas sesuai kebutuhan yang ditetapkan oleh Ketua Komite kepada Dewan Komisaris. Pada tahun 2024, Komite Audit telah menjadi rapat sebanyak 8 kali, dengan rincian sebagai berikut.

3. Involving independent parties outside the Audit Committee as necessary to assist in the performance of its duties (if needed).  
4. Exercising other authorities granted by the Board of Commissioners.

# Implementation of Duties

The Audit Committee has carried out its duties and responsibilities effectively and efficiently throughout 2024, as outlined below.

1. Reviewing the Company's Quarterly and Annual Financial Statements.  
2. Supervising the internal control system and risk management.  
3. Reviewing findings from the Internal Audit Unit and monitoring follow-up recommendations on these audit findings.  
4. Preparing and submitting work reports and recommendations to the President Commissioner.  
5. Conducting comprehensive oversight of GCG implementation, including monitoring potential conflicts of interest between the company's organs.

# Meeting

The Audit Committee holds an internal meeting at least once every 3 months or as required by the Chairman of the Committee or the Board of Commissioners. In 2024, the Audit Committee has held a meeting as many as 8 times, with the following details.

# KOMITE NOMINASI DAN REMUNERASI

NOMINATION AND REMUNERATION COMMITTEE

Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi berperan untuk melaksanan kebujakan nominasi dan remunerasi bagi Dewan Komisaris, Direksi, dan karyawan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Pedoman kerja Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi merujuk pada Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 34/ POJK.04/2014 tersebut Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik.

# Komposisi dan Masa Jabatan

Pada tahun 2024, terjadi perubahan dalam komposisi Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi, dengan penunjukan anggotabaru, Bapak Franky Henri Kawuka, yang menjabat di posisi managerial di bawah Direksi yang membidangi sumber daya manusia (SDM). Perubahan ini memastikan kepada komposisi komite tetap sesuai dengan kebanyak yang berlaku, dengan terdiri dari 1 Ketua yang bersal dari Komisaris Independen, serta 2 anggota eksternal yang memiliki keahlian di bidang SDM, manajemen, dan keuangan. Masa jabatan Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi disesuaikan denganASA jabatan Dewan Komisaris dan dapat diberhentikanapan sama sebelum matajabatan berakhir.

The Nomination and Remuneration Committee plays a role in implementing the nomination and remuneration policy for the Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, and employees.

# Work Guidelines

The working guidelines of the Nomination and Remuneration Committee refer to the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 34/POJK.04/2014 regarding the Nomination and Remuneration Committee of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Composition and Term of Office

In 2024, there is a change in the composition of the Nomination and Remuneration Committee, with the appointment of a new member, Mr. Franky Henri Kawuka, who holds a managerial position under the Board of Directors in the field of human resources (SDM). This change ensures that the composition of the committee remains in accordance with the applicable policies, consisting of 1 Chairman from the Independent Commissioner, as well as 2 external members who have expertise in the fields of human resources, management, and finance. The term of office of the Nomination and Remuneration Committee is adjusted to the term of office of the Board of Commissioners and can be dismissed at any time before the term of office ends.

# Independensi

Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi Perseroan menjadi independensinya dalam melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab tanpa intervensi dari pihak manapun. Keputusan yang diambil selelu bersifat objektif dan transparan, dengan mengutamakan kepada orang jangka panjang Perseroan. Independensi ini juga tercérmin dalam pemenuhan aspek-aspek independensi yang dijelaskan sebagai berikut.

# Independence

The Company's Nomination and Remuneration Committee maintains its independence in carrying out its duties and responsibilities without intervention from any party. The decisions taken are always objective and transparent, prioritizing the Company's long-term interests. This independence is also reflected in the fulfillment of the aspects of independence which are described as follows.
